<rate>2< /rate>< Review>
Reviews for this place are questionable at best. It's a cheaper version of Panda Express. The orange chicken was fine but the oil they used wasn't fresh by any means and the sauce was definitely sweet but lacked any serious flavor. The broccoli beef was fine but the broccoli was overcooked and cut haphazardly making for some awkward side-of-the-mouth bites.

They heap the thick-noodle chowmein on, but it's just mediocre too. Everything here is was you might expect with the added twist of being a little too affordable.  I'd go back if I only had ten dollars in my wallet and refused to eat from the nearby fast food places.<//Review>

<pictures>None</pictures><date>1522272708105< /date><userid>102651684007308117541</userid><user_name>Lifestyle Collective</user_name><Review>If there was a way to give negative stars, I'd completely rate this establishment with a negative 5 star rating. Where do I begin, is it the badly over prepared chicken tenders my son had, which nearly chipped his tooth (exaggerating, but nevertheless that's how over cooked they were) or is it the microwaved french fries that were deep fried to hide their freezer burned taste. It quite possibly could have been the wanna be latin hipster model bartender who thinks he's a tough guy for talking down at a customer who simple was asking for a drink the server had yet to bring after 20mins of waiting (not over exaggerating that part, bartender nor wait).

I find it very disappointing that this Applebee's was very unprepared as a staff and operating business. The kitchen made several mistakes throughout our order and just sitting at our booth observing the room, it seemed to be, we weren't the only group who had a lack luster experience.

Fortunately, the manager and our server had some decency about them and attempted to correct the issue. However, that time came and went with Mr tough guy at the bar. They did decide to comp the chicken fingers and drink, which was considerate of them. But, by far, the reputation and experience had already been damaged.

If you happen to find yourself at this location, tred carefully at the bar, confrontational wannabe model may try to spike your drink or may just have you waiting aimlessly. If you dare choose to sit, beware of the teeth chipping chicken fingers and long delays with a lost staff who jist may need an overhual in efficiency... probably starting with the kitchen.

So... all in all, Applebee's never go back... not worth the unfulfilled hunger and hassle. Hopefully this helps someone before it's too late!<//Review>< resp>

<user_name>Ann's Simply Delicious Recipes</user_name><Time>1409905836707</Time><Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
This review is long overdue, sorry about that!
On August 17th, 2014, my Honey and I set out for an early dinner. My appetite was leaning towards Applebee‚Äôs.

I had informed my husband that they had added some healthy choices to their menu since the last time we made a visit. Early this year we were unable to stay and dine because there were no choices of interest for him. So I was pretty sure that this time he would find something.

The host greeted us in a timely fashion. I asked the greeter if my husband could please view one of the menus before seating us, and that was no problem.
He did find a few things to his amazement.

We were escorted to a nice area of the restaurant, and quickly greeted by our wait.
A very cheerful young man approached our table and introduced himself as Robert. I have to say that his eagerness made me feel good and put a big smile on my face! I love it when waits are so cheery-eerie. We had a few questions regarding one of the entrees, so Robert took the initiative to go and ask one of his managers to come over and speak with us.

Within a minute we were greeted by Brittany, who had a bubbly outgoing personality. She explained that however, we wanted to substitute rice for more vegetables or another selection that they do their best to accommodate their customers. Their aim is to make sure that customers have a good experience and return.

My husband made a special request for more veggies in place of rice with his entree. Robert placed our order, and shortly after he walked away another manager approached our table and announced that the order would be coming right up; ‚ÄúIn fact sir, I will prepare it for you to make sure that it is just the way you like it!

Long story short, when Robert returned with the food everything was perfect. The veggies were crisp just as he likes them and the portion was huge. The grilled chicken was melt in your mouth and seasoned to perfection! I had the Bourbon steak and it was equally prepared to my liking.

I must say, the food was delicious and we were treated like royalty!
The staff is fantastic at this location. The two managers, Armando and Brittany go far beyond their call of duty to give the best in customer service. Our wait, Robert, was extremely accommodating, delightful and polite.

Thank you all for such an awesome experience. Corporate is most fortunate to have you as employees!  Keep up the great work!

Chef Ann< /Review>
